<div id="page6-div" style="position:relative;width:892px;height:1262px;">
<img width="892" height="1262" src="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/target006.png" alt="background image">
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft60">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft60">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:608px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft60">Introduction to Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;6</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:290px;left:116px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft61">•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:308px;left:161px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft610">•<br>•<br>•<br>•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:398px;left:116px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft61">•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:416px;left:161px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft610">•<br>•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:470px;left:116px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft610">•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:155px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft62">1&nbsp;&nbsp;Introduction to Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:200px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft610">Welcome to the Qu Data Export API. This document details the interfaces and standard use cases for integration&nbsp;<br>partners looking to leverage general data from Qu.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:245px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft610">The Data Export API is a&nbsp;<i>read-only</i>&nbsp;API that enables partners to retrieve raw data for analytics and post-processing&nbsp;<br>for the following core data sets:</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:290px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft64"><b>Check data</b>&nbsp;to retrieve check-level data including:</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:308px;left:175px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft610">Item sales<br>Service charges<br>Taxes<br>Payments<br>Voids and refunds</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:398px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft64"><b>Configuration data</b>&nbsp;to retrieve definitions and listings of major data sets including:</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:416px;left:175px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft610">Menu item, portion, groupings and category details<br>Ancillary data for taxes, payments, service charges and location details<br>Employee data for job , payroll profile and labor hours</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:470px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft610"><b>Till Reconciliation, Paid in/out, Over/Under data</b>&nbsp;and other financial balancing data<br><b>Employee/Labor data</b>&nbsp;for retrieving employee information and time clock data</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:515px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft610">The high level functions listed above encompass most of the currently available data, but more data points are&nbsp;<br>added frequently (or removed much less frequently) in any given release, so it is important to continually keep up&nbsp;<br>to date with release notes and check for changes to the data output.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:578px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft61">Please reach out to&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:578px;left:208px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft65"><a href="mailto:partnersupport@qubeyond.com">partnersupport@qubeyond.com</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:578px;left:412px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft61">&nbsp;if there are any questions, comments or feedback on this&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:596px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft61">documentation.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:646px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft66">1.1&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:646px;left:127px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft67">Resources</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:698px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft68">1.1.1&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:698px;left:139px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft69">Base URLs</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:741px;left:171px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft64"><b>Staging/Sandbox URL</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:741px;left:535px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft64"><b>Production/Live URL</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:785px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft65"><a href="https://reporting-api-stg.qubeyond.com/">https://reporting-api-stg.qubeyond.com</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:785px;left:425px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft65"><a href="https://reporting-api.qubeyond.com/">https://reporting-api.qubeyond.com</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:847px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft68">1.1.2&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:847px;left:139px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft69">Request and response structure</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:880px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft610">The Qu API is organized around REST with predictable, resource-oriented URLs and HTTP response codes to&nbsp;<br>indicate API errors. Every request to Qu is comprised of HTTP Headers, endpoint URL and (for some requests) a&nbsp;<br>JSON Body. All JSON structures follow the rules specified in RFC4627; and are encoded as UTF8 as specified in&nbsp;<br>RFC3629 using one to four bytes per Unicode code point.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:961px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft61">All responses return in JSON format and uses standard HTTP response codes for ease of development.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1004px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft68">1.1.3&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1004px;left:139px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft69">Required HTTP headers</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1037px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft61">All requests to Qu APIs must include the following headers:</p>
</div>

<img width="892" height="1262" src="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/target007.png" alt="background image">
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft70">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft70">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:608px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft70">Introduction to Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;7</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft71"><b>Header</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:329px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft71"><b>Format</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:606px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft71"><b>Description</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:206px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft71"><b>Authorization</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:210px;left:236px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft72">Bearer &lt;JWT Token&gt;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:206px;left:501px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft710">Use generated token during initial&nbsp;<br>authentication.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:251px;left:501px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft74"><i>Note: Not required in the initial authentication request.</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:301px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft71"><b>X-Integration</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:304px;left:236px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft72">&lt;decoded qu.uid string&gt;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:301px;left:501px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft73">See section below for more detail.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:370px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft75">Generating the&nbsp;<b>X-Integration header</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:404px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft73">The X-Integration header should be set as the&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:404px;left:376px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft72">qu.uid</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:404px;left:434px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft73">&nbsp;of the decoded JWT token received when authenticating&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:426px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft710">for Qu services. This JWT is encoded via the HS256 algorithm. There are many resources and libraries available&nbsp;<br><a href="https://jwt.io/libraries">online for decoding JWTs and parsing data, Qu recommends&nbsp;</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:444px;left:465px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft77"><a href="https://jwt.io/libraries">https://jwt.io/libraries</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:444px;left:604px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft73"><a href="https://jwt.io/libraries">&nbsp;as a starting point.</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:837px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft71"><b>1&nbsp;Decoded Qu token example via http://jwt.io</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:887px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft78">1.2&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:887px;left:127px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft79">Authentication</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:923px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft710">Authentication to the API is performed via OAuth. To perform requests, it is required to authenticate with the&nbsp;<br>credentials of a user that belongs to a company.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:979px;left:171px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft71"><b>Staging/Sandbox URL</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:979px;left:535px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft71"><b>Production/Live URL</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1022px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft77"><a href="https://auth-stg.qubeyond.com/api/v3.5/token">https://auth-stg.qubeyond.com/api/v3.5/token</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1022px;left:425px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft77"><a href="https://auth.qubeyond.com/api/v3.5/token">https://auth.qubeyond.com/api/v3.5/token</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1059px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft71"><b>Sample request:</b></p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:506px;left:102px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft82">&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:506px;left:134px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft83">"companyId"</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:506px;left:223px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft82">:&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:506px;left:239px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft86">111</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:524px;left:102px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft82">}</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:557px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft81">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:607px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft87">1.3&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:607px;left:127px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft88">Endpoint and parameters</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:643px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft818">There is only 1 endpoint for the Data Export API, and all data requests are made using parameters to identify the&nbsp;<br>sub-type and filtering properties to receive.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:688px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft81">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:765px;left:135px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft89">companyId</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:765px;left:220px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft81">&nbsp;is the customer's unique account ID in Qu, which will always be the same for any given&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:787px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft81">location.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:809px;left:135px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft89">locationId</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:809px;left:229px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft81">&nbsp;is the unique location Id (store) for which the data will be retrieved. These location IDs can&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:831px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft81">be provided by the brand or Qu account representative or can be&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:831px;left:537px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft810"><a href="https://qubeyond.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/INT/pages/1117913138/Available+Locations#Listing-available-locations">retrieved using the API</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:831px;left:678px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft81">&nbsp;itself.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:858px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft81">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:973px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft811">1.3.1&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:973px;left:139px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft812">Request parameters</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1006px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft819">There are several parameters that can be used for refining and filtering the data retrieved from the API. Not all&nbsp;<br>parameters are relevant to each scenario, a list of valid parameters will be provided in each major data section&nbsp;<br>along with best practices.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1079px;left:150px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft84"><b>Parameter</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1079px;left:508px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft84"><b>Description</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:727px;left:97px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft813"><b>GET</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:727px;left:123px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft81">&nbsp;<i><b>/api/v3.5/export/{companyId}/{locationid}</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:898px;left:129px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft818">The API access credentials provided will only work for a single customerId, but can be used for all&nbsp;<br>locationIds within that customerId.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:895px;left:99px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft815"></p>
</div>

<div id="page9-div" style="position:relative;width:892px;height:1262px;">
<img width="892" height="1262" src="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/target009.png" alt="background image">
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft90">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft90">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:608px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft90">Introduction to Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;9</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:165px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft91"><i><b>data_type&nbsp;</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:165px;left:171px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft92"><b>MANDATORY</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft93"><b>Mandatory. Values:&nbsp;</b><i>config, checks, labor, paid_inout, over_under, tills, desposits.</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:189px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft95">Specifies the type of data to export.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:235px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft91"><i><b>start_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:235px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft97"><b>Mandatory</b>&nbsp;for&nbsp;<i>checks, labor, paid_inout, over_under</i>, and&nbsp;<i>tills</i>.&nbsp;<b>Optional</b>&nbsp;for&nbsp;<br><i>config.</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:280px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft95">Start date of the export.&nbsp;<b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:326px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft91"><i><b>end_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:326px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft95">End date of the export.&nbsp;<b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:372px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft91"><i><b>sub_data_type</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:372px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft98"><b>Values:&nbsp;</b><i>category, item_group, item, portion, void_reason, discount, tax,&nbsp;<br>service_charge, payment_type, employee, job, paid_inout, location, order_type,&nbsp;<br>order_channel, day_part, payroll_profile, time_entry_reason.</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:435px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft97">Configuration data type can also be further categorized by different sub types,&nbsp;<br>e.g. Discounts. For details see&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:453px;left:483px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft96"><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html"><i>Configuration data sub types and use cases</i></a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:453px;left:748px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft95"><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html">.&nbsp;</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:500px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft91"><i><b>delta_from_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:527px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft91"><i><b>delta_from_time</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:500px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft97">Each response contains&nbsp;<b>delta</b>&nbsp;response parameters. If the next request contains&nbsp;<br><b>delta</b>&nbsp;parameters instead of&nbsp;<b>start_date</b>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<b>end_date</b>&nbsp;then response will&nbsp;<br>contain data added since time defined in&nbsp;<b>delta</b>. Use for incremental export.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:582px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft91"><i><b>include_abandoned</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:582px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft93"><b>Values:</b><i>&nbsp;true, false</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:609px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft93"><b>Applies to:&nbsp;</b><i>data_type=checks</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:636px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft97"><i>IncludeAbandoned</i>&nbsp;parameter is only used when requesting checks&nbsp;<br>(<i>data_type=checks</i>). When set to "true", the response will include all the checks&nbsp;<br>with state “Abandoned” for the requested location and date ranges.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:699px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft97">All shifts, tills and checks that were left open by the employees will be processed&nbsp;<br>by an automatic task that runs everyday after the business hours of each&nbsp;<br>location. This process can be enabled or disabled depending on the customer&nbsp;<br>preferences.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:780px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft95">Checks that are processed by this task are set to state "Abandoned".</p>
</div>

<div id="page10-div" style="position:relative;width:892px;height:1262px;">
<img width="892" height="1262" src="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/target010.png" alt="background image">
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft100">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft100">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:601px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft100">Introduction to Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;10</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:216px;left:306px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft105">•<br>•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:513px;left:300px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft101">1.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:549px;left:300px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft101">2.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:585px;left:300px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft101">3.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:621px;left:345px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft101">a.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:639px;left:344px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft101">b.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:657px;left:345px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft101">c.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft102"><i><b>output_structure</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft103"><b>Values</b>:&nbsp;<i>item_portion_unified / default</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:189px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft103"><b>Applies to:</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:216px;left:320px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft106"><i>data_type=checks<br>data_type=config&amp;sub_data_type=item<br>data_type=config&amp;sub_data_type=item_group</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:279px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft105">The&nbsp;<i>output_structure</i>&nbsp;parameter was introduced to support the unify item-<br>portion id representation, on each configuration (item / item_group) and also&nbsp;<br>on the checks response.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:342px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft105">In case we send a default or empty value the response will contain the items and&nbsp;<br>portions separately as usual .</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:387px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft105">When set the value as&nbsp;<i>item_portion_unified</i>&nbsp;it will return a combination of the&nbsp;<br>items and portions with a unique item id representing the item-portion id. In&nbsp;<br>this case the portion id won’t be exported and the name of the new item will&nbsp;<br>contain the portion description.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:468px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft105">Consider the following example - an&nbsp; item “Mac &amp; Cheese” with portions&nbsp;<br>“Regular” and “Large”The conversion consists in 3 steps:</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:513px;left:320px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft105">For each Portion that “Mac &amp; Cheese” had configured, a new individual item&nbsp;<br>was created.<br>A new unique ID is generated for each new item (this ID is only visible on the&nbsp;<br>API for now).<br>The names for the new items are a combination of the Item’s and its&nbsp;<br>Portion’s names.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:621px;left:365px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft105">Item: “Mac &amp; Cheese”<br>Portion: “Regular”<br>New Item: “Mac &amp; Cheese, Regular”&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:684px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft105">Combined names will be visible only when exporting 'config/item'. Exporting&nbsp;<br>'config/item_group' and 'checks'&nbsp; will show only the new ids.&nbsp; Also if the items&nbsp;<br>do not have portions they will be converted as well creating new item_ids.</p>
</div>

<div id="page11-div" style="position:relative;width:892px;height:1262px;">
<img width="892" height="1262" src="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/target011.png" alt="background image">
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft110">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft110">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:591px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft110">Working with the Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;11</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:353px;left:116px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft1111">•<br>•<br>•<br>•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:155px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft112">2&nbsp;&nbsp;Working with the Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:200px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft1111">The Data Export API is an extremely versatile API designed to be used for a variety of applications. Because of this,&nbsp;<br>rather than exhaustively try to identify each use case, this guide seeks to provide best practices and strategies for&nbsp;<br>the consumption of the data retrieved to get the most out of the functions.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:263px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft1111">As such, high level use cases for each major category have been created along with the spec itself. It is up to the&nbsp;<br>integrator to responsibly manipulate the data themselves as the exported data provided from this API is raw and&nbsp;<br>does not include summaries or aggregations.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:326px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft111">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:353px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft1112"><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html#page11-div">Available Locations Data<br></a><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html#page13-div">Check Data<br></a><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html#page34-div">Configuration Data<br></a><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html#page57-div">Employee and Labor Data<br></a><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html#page66-div">Accounting Data</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:475px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft114">2.1&nbsp;&nbsp;Available Locations Data</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:511px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft1111">Getting the list of available locations and information about each location is essential to know the location_id for&nbsp;<br>any location-specific requests.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:623px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft115">2.1.1&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:623px;left:139px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft116">Relevant parameters</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:656px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft111">(None)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:683px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft111">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:726px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft115">2.1.2&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:726px;left:139px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft116">Location object</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:769px;left:190px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft117"><b>Attribute&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:769px;left:565px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft117"><b>Type&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:815px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft118"><i>id</i></p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:833px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft136">2.2&nbsp;&nbsp;Check Data</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:869px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft1312">Check data is generally the most crucial data set that integrators make use of. The Data Export API provides a raw&nbsp;<br>feed of check data with a custom set of parameters to further refine what can become a firehose of data.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:981px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft131">2.2.1&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:981px;left:139px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft132">Relevant parameters</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1024px;left:127px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft138"><b>Parameter</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1024px;left:485px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft138"><b>Description</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:926px;left:97px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft139"><b>GET</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:926px;left:123px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft137">&nbsp;<i><b>/api/v3.5/export/{customerid}/{locationid}?data_type=checks</b></i></p>

<div id="page14-div" style="position:relative;width:892px;height:1262px;">
<img width="892" height="1262" src="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/target014.png" alt="background image">
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft140">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft140">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:591px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft140">Working with the Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;14</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft141"><i><b>start_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:189px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft142">(Basic)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft146">Specifies the starting point for the export. This will include all checks for this date and&nbsp;<br>onward until&nbsp;<b>end_date</b>&nbsp;(if applicable).</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:207px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft144"><i>This is mandatory if not using the&nbsp;<b>delta</b>&nbsp;parameters.</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:234px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft143"><b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:280px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft141"><i><b>end_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:307px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft142">(Basic)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:280px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft146">Specifies the end date for the export. If applied this will be the end of the date range and&nbsp;<br>include all checks up to and including this date.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:325px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft146">If&nbsp;<b>end_date</b>&nbsp;is not specified then the export will return all indexed checks up until the&nbsp;<br>moment that the request to the API was made.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:370px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft143"><b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:416px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft141"><i><b>delta_from_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:443px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft142">(Advanced)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:416px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft146">These parameters should only be used when doing incremental export updates&nbsp;<br>throughout the day such as for integrators updating data live. If using delta parameters,&nbsp;<br>do not use the startDate and endDate parameters.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:479px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft143"><b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY / HHMM</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:489px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft141"><i><b>delta_from_time</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:516px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft142">(Advanced)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:611px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft141"><i><b>include_abandoned</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:638px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft142">(Advanced)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:611px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft146"><i>IncludeAbandoned</i>&nbsp;parameter is only used when requesting checks (<i>data_type=checks</i>).&nbsp;<br>When set to "true", the response will include all the checks with state “Abandoned” for&nbsp;<br>the requested location and date ranges.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:674px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft146">All shifts, tills and checks that were left open by the employees will be processed by an&nbsp;<br>automatic task that runs everyday after the business hours of each location. This&nbsp;<br>process can be enabled or disabled depending on the customer preferences.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:737px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft142">Checks that are processed by this task are set to state "Abandoned".</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:764px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft143"><b>Format:</b><i>&nbsp;true, false</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:520px;left:292px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft146">Using the&nbsp;<b>delta</b>&nbsp;fields will return data that can be “volatile” in that the check&nbsp;<br>data could be altered after the initial polling and should always be reconciled&nbsp;<br>with a standard lookback request to ensure the data is complete.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:517px;left:262px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft145"></p>
</div>

<div id="page15-div" style="position:relative;width:892px;height:1262px;">
<img width="892" height="1262" src="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/target015.png" alt="background image">
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft150">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft150">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:591px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft150">Working with the Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;15</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:378px;left:252px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft151">1.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:414px;left:252px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft151">2.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:450px;left:252px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft151">3.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:486px;left:297px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft151">a.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:504px;left:296px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft151">b.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:522px;left:298px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft151">c.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:770px;left:116px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft158">•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft152"><i><b>output_structure</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:189px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft151">(Advanced)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft158">The&nbsp;<i>output_structure</i>&nbsp;parameter was introduced to support the unify item-portion id&nbsp;<br>representation, on each configuration (item / item_group) and also on the checks&nbsp;<br>response.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:225px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft158">In case we send a default or empty value the response will contain the items and&nbsp;<br>portions separately as usual .</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:270px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft158">When set the value as&nbsp;<i>item_portion_unified</i>&nbsp;it will return a combination of the items and&nbsp;<br>portions with a unique item id representing the item-portion id. In this case the portion&nbsp;<br>id won’t be exported and the name of the new item will contain the portion description.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:333px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft158">Consider the following example - an&nbsp; item “Mac &amp; Cheese” with portions “Regular” and&nbsp;<br>“Large”The conversion consists in 3 steps:</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:378px;left:273px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft158">For each Portion that “Mac &amp; Cheese” had configured, a new individual item was&nbsp;<br>created.<br>A new unique ID is generated for each new item (this ID is only visible on the API for&nbsp;<br>now).<br>The names for the new items are a combination of the Item’s and its Portion’s&nbsp;<br>names.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:486px;left:318px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft158">Item: “Mac &amp; Cheese”<br>Portion: “Regular”<br>New Item: “Mac &amp; Cheese, Regular”&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:549px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft158">Combined names will be visible only when exporting 'config/item'. Exporting 'config/<br>item_group' and 'checks'&nbsp; will show only the new ids.&nbsp; Also if the items do not have&nbsp;<br>portions they will be converted as well creating new item_ids.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:612px;left:248px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft154"><b>Values</b>:&nbsp;<i>item_portion_unified / default</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:674px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft155">2.2.2&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:674px;left:139px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft156">Check data strategies</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:707px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft158">The parameters above can be used for basic data retrieval as well as for more advanced applications. The basic and&nbsp;<br>advanced strategy references should be reviewed and it is recommended to discuss with a Qu technical contact on&nbsp;<br>which fields to make use of based on the individual use case for the integration.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:770px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft159"><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html#page28-div">Basic Check Data Strategies<br></a><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html#page30-div">Advanced Check Data Strategies</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:815px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft151">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:859px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft155">2.2.3&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:859px;left:139px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft156">Check object</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:902px;left:134px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft154"><b>Attribute</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:902px;left:305px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft154"><b>Type</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:902px;left:515px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft154"><b>Additional Information</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:946px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft151">check_id</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:946px;left:261px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft151">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:946px;left:404px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft158">Unique ID for the check. Use this ID for identifying specific&nbsp;<br>checks on external systems</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1010px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft151">check_guid</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1010px;left:261px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft151">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1010px;left:404px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft151">Alternate internal check ID</p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:662px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft286">2.2.5&nbsp;&nbsp;Basic Check Data Strategies</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:695px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft288">While the check data can be manipulated in so many ways by the integrator, there are a few key strategies that are&nbsp;<br>recommended for basic check logging and analytics.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:740px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft281">Basic check strategies are most relevant to integrators that:</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:767px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft288">Consume check data less frequently (once a day or less)<br>Do not use check sales data for intra-day reporting or “live” dashboards<br>Do not have specific considerations around portioning and inventory tracking<br>Do not track abandoned checks (a common item for loss prevention integrations)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:863px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft287">Implementing a basic check data collection strategy</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:893px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft281">The basic use cases are generally:</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:920px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft288">Getting check data for a specific day<br>Getting check data for a range of time<br>Getting all checks since a date</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:983px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft281">In these cases the standard request formats will be:</p>
</div>

<img width="892" height="1262" src="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/target029.png" alt="background image">
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft290">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft290">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:591px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft290">Working with the Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;29</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:206px;left:279px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft296">•<br>•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:315px;left:279px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft296">•<br>•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:424px;left:279px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft296">•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:551px;left:116px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft296">•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:767px;left:116px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:785px;left:161px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:821px;left:161px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:857px;left:161px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:893px;left:116px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:911px;left:161px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:947px;left:161px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:140px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft292"><b>Scenario</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:457px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft292"><b>Request parameters</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:206px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">Single Day</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:206px;left:293px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft296">data_type=checks<br>start_date={MMDDYYYY}<br>end_date={MMDDYYYY}</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:269px;left:268px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">Start and End date should be the same day in this scenario.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:315px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">Date Range</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:315px;left:293px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft296">data_type=checks<br>start_date={MMDDYYYY}<br>end_date={MMDDYYYY}</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:378px;left:268px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">Start and End date should be different in this scenario.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:424px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">All Checks Since</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:424px;left:293px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft296">data_type=checks<br>start_date={MMDDYYYY}</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:469px;left:268px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">Do not specify any end_date.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:524px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft293">Things to know about this strategy</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:551px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft296">Checks retrieved on these dates will be for the entire day’s worth of checks.<br>If the current date is included or the parameter does not include a past date as the end date, then all checks&nbsp;<br>up until the moment of the request will be included.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:623px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft291">Changes to check data after the fact</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:650px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft296">When requesting from a single date or a range of dates, the most recent “iteration” of the check data will always be&nbsp;<br>returned. This is an especially important concept to understand when dealing with both basic and advanced&nbsp;<br>strategies and is best illustrated with an example.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:713px;left:102px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft297"><i>Scenario: a check is created on&nbsp;<b>September 1st</b>&nbsp;with 3 items. The following day (9/2), the check is re-opened and 2 of&nbsp;<br>the items are refunded. The day after that (9/3), the check is re-opened again and the last item is refunded, resulting&nbsp;<br>in a $0 check.</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:767px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft292"><b>Using Strategy 1:</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:785px;left:175px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft296">If the application fetches all checks for starting and ending date of&nbsp;<b>9/1</b>: the check will have 3 items on&nbsp;<br>it and no refunds logged<br>If the application fetches all checks for starting and ending date of&nbsp;<b>9/2</b>: the check will appear with a&nbsp;<br>refund of two items (and not including the 3rd item that was still settled)<br>If the application fetches all checks for the starting and ending date of&nbsp;<b>9/3</b>: the check will appear with&nbsp;<br>the last item refunded</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:893px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft292"><b>Using Strategy 2:</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:911px;left:175px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft296">If the application fetches all checks for the range of&nbsp;<b>9/1 - 9/2:&nbsp;</b>the check will appear with a refund of&nbsp;<br>two items (and not including the 3rd item that was still settled)<br>If the application fetches all checks for the range of&nbsp;<b>9/1 - 9/3</b>: the check will appear with all items&nbsp;<br>refunded</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:992px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft292"><b>Why is it like this?</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1019px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft296">When a check is created in the system, it is immediately saved to the cloud as is. When changes occur, a new version&nbsp;<br>of the check is published and the previous version is logged as a child data set within the check. This allows for&nbsp;<br>consistency in daily reporting so it is possible to look up a previous day and see what the exact conditions were at&nbsp;<br>the time of closing on that day, without conflating it with changes that occurred later on.</p>
</div>

<div id="page30-div" style="position:relative;width:892px;height:1262px;">
<img width="892" height="1262" src="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/target030.png" alt="background image">
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft300">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft300">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:591px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft300">Working with the Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;30</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:444px;left:116px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:480px;left:161px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft301">•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:498px;left:116px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft301">•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:805px;left:316px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">•<br>•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:914px;left:316px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">•<br>•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:152px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">This scenario of a check being re-opened and refunded separately across 3 different days is an incredibly unlikely&nbsp;<br>scenario, but it illustrates that the specific date that is requested will not always be the most complete view of the&nbsp;<br>check, and that the status can change over time based on the configuration of the&nbsp;given brand.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:339px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft302">2.2.6&nbsp;&nbsp;Advanced Check Data Strategies</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:372px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">While the check data can be manipulated in so many ways by the integrator, there are a few key strategies that are&nbsp;<br>recommended for basic check logging and analytics.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:417px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft301">Advanced check strategies are most relevant to integrators that:</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:444px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">Consume check frequently throughout the day for semi-live reporting, analytics or insights<br>Use item data from checks to inform inventory management platforms</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:480px;left:175px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft301">Especially where there are portion-specific “recipes” mapped on the current IMS design</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:498px;left:130px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft301">Track abandoned checks (a common item for loss prevention integrations)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:541px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft303">Implementing advanced check data collection strategies by use case</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:580px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft304">Get incremental check data throughout the day</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:607px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">The Qu Data Export API does not currently support data-streaming, so all intra-day updates have to be polled from&nbsp;<br>the integrator-side. While there are no hard limits on the frequency, It is generally recommended to set this cadence&nbsp;<br>to no more than every 15 minutes, even for live dashboards as there’s diminishing returns on the relevance of the&nbsp;<br>telemetry, and shorter frequencies can lead to other issues as checks are most likely to be reopened and edited&nbsp;<br>within the first 10 minutes of ordering, and significantly less after that.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:706px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft309">No matter the frequency, the way to get incremental check data throughout the day is to use the&nbsp;<b>delta_from_date<br></b>and&nbsp;<b>delta_from_time</b>&nbsp;properties instead of the standard startDate and endDate properties.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:761px;left:158px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft305"><b>Scenario</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:761px;left:355px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft305"><b>Request parameters</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:761px;left:664px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft305"><b>Result</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:805px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">Placing a request at 2:00PM&nbsp;<br>on October 1st for checks&nbsp;<br>from the last 15 minutes</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:805px;left:330px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">data_type=checks<br>delta_from_date={10012022}<br>delta_from_time={1345}</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:868px;left:305px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft301">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:805px;left:577px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">A list of checks between 1:45PM&nbsp;<br>and the current moment (2:00PM).</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:914px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">Placing a request at 2:00PM&nbsp;<br>on October 1st for checks&nbsp;<br>from the last&nbsp;<b>5 DAYS</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:914px;left:330px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">data_type=checks<br>delta_from_date={09262022}<br>delta_from_time={1400}</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:914px;left:577px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">A list of checks starting at 2:00PM&nbsp;<br>on September 26th and going up to&nbsp;<br>the current moment (2:00PM)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:228px;left:129px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft308">It is&nbsp;<b>highly recommended&nbsp;</b>that any integrator that consumes check data for use that includes tracking the&nbsp;<br>voiding or refunding of checks implement ”lookback” logic that retrieves historical check data from a&nbsp;<br>period of multiple previous days with logic to overwrite previously stored check data if it is found there are&nbsp;<br>changes to the check. Failure to do so&nbsp;<b>will</b>&nbsp;result in erroneous final data collection.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:225px;left:99px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft306"></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1005px;left:129px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft309">The second scenario above, while possible, is&nbsp;<b>highly discouraged</b>&nbsp;as it will return all check data changes&nbsp;<br>within that time period which could return multiple instances of checks and have other inconsistent&nbsp;<br>results.&nbsp;<b>For anything that spans more than a day, the proper use should be the basic start and end&nbsp;<br>date format from the&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1059px;left:271px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft307"><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html"><b>basic check strategy</b></a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1059px;left:405px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft305"><b>.</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1002px;left:99px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft306"></p>
</div>

<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft310">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft310">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:591px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft310">Working with the Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;31</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:152px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft311">Set up custom IDs for portion-specific recipes</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:179px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft3111">Many brands make use of Qu portions, which exist as a property of the item itself and not as an actual item. For&nbsp;<br>example a small soda is simple a soda with the portion property of small. The small portion can then be re-used for&nbsp;<br>any item, not just sodas. This can present challenges for integrators that maintain atomic portioned items in their&nbsp;<br>database for reference as there is no uniqueness to the Item Master ID provided or the portion used.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:260px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft3111">As a way to make this transition easier, Qu has a parameter that allows for the specification of items x portions as&nbsp;<br>unique IDs so that they can be mapped uniquely on the receiving database rather than through parsing logic.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:305px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft3111">When the parameter&nbsp;<b>“output_structure”</b>&nbsp;is set to&nbsp;<i><b>item_portion_unified</b></i>, the returned item data will have&nbsp;<br>automatically generated IDs for all item x portion combinations in the check data which can then be directly related&nbsp;<br>to the recipe on the integrator side.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:368px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft312">Here’s an example with the&nbsp;<b>default</b>&nbsp;item output as compared to the<b>&nbsp;item_portion_unified</b>&nbsp;option.</p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:782px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft336">Track abandoned checks</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:809px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft338">Abandoned checks are defined within Qu as a check that has been started and has content on it but has not been&nbsp;<br>paid for by the time the end of day report is run. When the EOD process runs, it will force any unpaid checks into the&nbsp;<br>abandoned state to remove them from the suspended check list so that no checks remain unaccounted for in the&nbsp;<br>check data.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:899px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft332">How are abandoned checks created?</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:926px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft338">These checks are created when a check is suspended by the cashier, either as a “shortcut” to voiding all the items&nbsp;<br>on an order cancelled before being fully paid or as a way to put a check aside while a guest goes to do something&nbsp;<br>else such as get their wallet from the car. Occasionally it can also indicate training issues or worse, theft, since the&nbsp;<br>check can still be sent to the kitchen for processing.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1007px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft338">By default, abandoned checks are filtered out in the Data API export or in Qu’s EI reporting views as they do not&nbsp;<br>count as paid and closed checks. To keep them in results, include the parameter “include_abandoned=true” in the&nbsp;<br>API request.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:678px;left:129px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft338">The use of this parameter to generate these unique IDs is consistent and will not change over time for any&nbsp;<br>specific item x portion mapping unless one of those IDs is altered.<br>However the ID is not currently available for review within the Qu platform, the structure only exists in the&nbsp;<br>Data Export API translation layer.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:675px;left:99px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft337"></p>
</div>

<p style="position:absolute;top:396px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft343">2.3&nbsp;&nbsp;Configuration Data</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:432px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft3412">Configuration data is used as a reference for understanding and displaying properties received from Check, Labor&nbsp;<br>and Accounting data.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:524px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft3412">Use of Configuration Data will depend on the data that the integrator will be exporting and is separated into&nbsp;<br><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html">relevant sub types for ease of access. See&nbsp;</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:542px;left:344px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft344"><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html">Configuration data sub types and use cases</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:542px;left:615px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft341"><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html">&nbsp;below for details.</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:585px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft345">2.3.1&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:585px;left:139px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft346">Relevant parameters</p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:674px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft341">The various data references available.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:701px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft342"><b>Values:&nbsp;</b><i>(see section below)</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:747px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft347"><i><b>output_structure</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:774px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft341">(Advanced)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:747px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft3412">The&nbsp;<i>output_structure</i>&nbsp;parameter was introduced to support the unify item-portion id&nbsp;<br>representation, on each configuration (item / item_group) and also on the checks&nbsp;<br>response. See&nbsp;</p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:801px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft341">output_structure parameter.</p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:918px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft345">2.3.2&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:918px;left:139px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft346">Configuration data sub types and use cases</p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:589px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft516">2.3.13&nbsp;&nbsp;Day Part</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:622px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft517">A&nbsp;<i>day part</i>&nbsp;is a segment of the day. Breakfast, lunch, and dinner schedules can be set using&nbsp;<i>day parts</i>.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:649px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft517">This request provides all&nbsp;<i>day parts</i>&nbsp;for the selected location:</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:742px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft512"><i>Day part</i>&nbsp;object&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:782px;left:145px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft519"><b>Attribute&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:782px;left:332px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft519"><b>Type&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:782px;left:542px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft519"><b>Additional Information&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:829px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft518"><i>id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:829px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft517">long</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:829px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft517">ID of the&nbsp;<i>day part.</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:875px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft518"><i>name</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:875px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft517">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:879px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft517">Name set to the&nbsp;<i>day part</i>&nbsp;(<i>e.g.,</i>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:879px;left:636px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5110">"Breakfast"</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:879px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft517">)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:929px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft518"><i>start_time</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:929px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft517">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:932px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft517">Start time of the to the&nbsp;<i>day part (e.g.,&nbsp;</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:932px;left:678px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5110">"3:00AM"</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:932px;left:754px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft518"><i>)</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:982px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft518"><i>end_time</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:982px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft517">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:986px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft517">End time of the to the&nbsp;<i>day part (e.g.,&nbsp;</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:986px;left:671px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5110">"10:00AM"</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:986px;left:757px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft518"><i>)</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:688px;left:97px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5111"><b>GET&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:688px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5112"><i><b>/api/v3.5/export/{customerid}/{locationid}?data_type=config&amp;sub_data_type=day_part</b></i></p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:589px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft536">2.3.15&nbsp;&nbsp;Time Entry Reason</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:622px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5314">Some customer configurations will require that an employee sets a reason for clocking in or out, or when taking a&nbsp;<br>break. These reasons can be customized per customer, and will be included with any Labor activity if applicable.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:733px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft532"><i>Time&nbsp;entry reason</i>&nbsp;object&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:773px;left:145px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft538"><b>Attribute&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:773px;left:332px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft538"><b>Type&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:773px;left:542px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft538"><b>Additional Information&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:820px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft539"><i>id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:820px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft537">long</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:820px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft537">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:866px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft539"><i>title</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:866px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft537">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:866px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft537">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:912px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft539"><i>type</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:912px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft537">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:916px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft537">&nbsp;Values can be either&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:916px;left:577px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5310">PAID</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:916px;left:617px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft537">&nbsp;or&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:916px;left:641px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5310">UNPAID</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:916px;left:700px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft537">.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:679px;left:97px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5311"><b>GET&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:679px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5312"><i><b>/api/v3.5/export/{customerid}/{locationid}?data_type=config&amp;sub_data_type=time_entry_reason</b></i></p>
</div>

<p style="position:absolute;top:769px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft546">2.3.16&nbsp;&nbsp;Paid In/Out Reason</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:802px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft547">Customers often require a specific reason for a pay-in or pay-out, which is listed uniquely in Qu for retrieval.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:895px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft542"><i>Paid in/out reason</i>&nbsp;object&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:935px;left:137px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft548"><b>Attribute&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:935px;left:302px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft548"><b>Type&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:935px;left:520px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft548"><b>Additional Information&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:982px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft549"><i>id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:982px;left:261px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft547">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:982px;left:398px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft547">Unique for every entry.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1028px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft549"><i>name</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1028px;left:261px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft547">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1028px;left:398px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft547">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:841px;left:97px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5410"><b>GET&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:841px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5411"><i><b>/api/v3.5/export/{customerid}/{locationid}?data_type=config&amp;sub_data_type=paid_inout</b></i></p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:602px;left:102px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5711">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; },<br>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; {<br>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:638px;left:215px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft575">34</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:638px;left:231px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft573">,</p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:656px;left:215px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft573">:&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:656px;left:231px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft574">"Medium Rare"</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:674px;left:102px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5711">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; },<br>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ...<br>&nbsp; &nbsp; ]<br>&nbsp; }<br>}</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:811px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft576">2.4&nbsp;&nbsp;Employee and Labor Data</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:847px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5712">Employee and Labor data is used primarily by HRIS systems to pull relevant employee information as well as clock&nbsp;<br>in/out records and breaks. This read-only data is often used in conjunction with the Qu Labor API to allow employee&nbsp;<br>management functions and tracking.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:927px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft578">2.4.1&nbsp;&nbsp;Employee</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:960px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5712">A Qu Employee object contains relevant data for each employee for the given location. This includes specific job&nbsp;<br>titles and payroll profiles for the given location.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1005px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft5712">Qu does not store high-risk PII such as SSN or EIN and in fact it is encouraged to limit the amount of PII that is&nbsp;<br>provided for integration partners that use the Qu Labor API to manage employees outside of the Qu platform.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1062px;left:97px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft579"><b>GET</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1062px;left:123px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft577">&nbsp;<i><b>/api/v3.5/export/{customerid}/{locationid}?data_type=config&amp;sub_data_type=employee</b></i></p>
</div>

<img width="892" height="1262" src="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/target061.png" alt="background image">
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft610">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft610">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:591px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft610">Working with the Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;61</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:539px;left:488px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft619">•<br>•<br>•<br>•</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:153px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft612">2.4.2&nbsp;&nbsp;Payroll Profile</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:186px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft619">The Payroll Profile is a reusable object in the Qu system that defines how wages are calculated for each employee&nbsp;<br>for a given job. For systems that rely on Qu-originated wage and clock in/out records, the Payroll Profile is one of&nbsp;<br>the most important pieces to reconciling that information.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:316px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft613"><i>Payroll profile</i>&nbsp;object&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:356px;left:163px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft615"><b>Attribute&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:356px;left:368px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft615"><b>Type&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:356px;left:599px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft615"><b>Description</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:402px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft616"><i>id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:402px;left:315px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">long</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:402px;left:477px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:448px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft616"><i>name</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:448px;left:315px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:448px;left:477px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:494px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft616"><i>payroll_type</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:494px;left:315px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:494px;left:477px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft619">A mandatory identifier used for grouping payroll&nbsp;<br>profiles. Can be 1 of 4 types:</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:539px;left:502px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft619">Hourly, with overtime<br>Hourly, no overtime<br>Salaried, with overtime<br>Salaried, no overtime</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:639px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft616"><i>calculate_weekly</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:639px;left:315px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">bool</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:639px;left:477px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft619">Whether the employee’s hours have a weekly limit&nbsp;<br>before overtime applies.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:703px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft616"><i>weekly_hours</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:703px;left:315px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">int</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:703px;left:477px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">Hours allowed per week before overtime kicks in.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:750px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft616"><i>calculate_daily</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:750px;left:315px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">bool</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:750px;left:477px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft619">Whether the employee’s hours have a daily limit&nbsp;<br>before overtime applies.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:814px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft616"><i>daily_hours</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:814px;left:315px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">int</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:814px;left:477px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">Hours allowed per day before overtime kicks in.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:860px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft616"><i>double_daily_hours</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:860px;left:315px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">int</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:860px;left:477px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft619">Hours allowed per day before double overtime&nbsp;<br>kicks in.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:924px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft616"><i>overtime_multiplier</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:924px;left:315px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">decimal</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:924px;left:477px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">Multiplier applied to wage for overtime worked.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:970px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft616"><i>double_overtime_multiplier</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:970px;left:315px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">decimal</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:970px;left:477px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft619">Multiplier applied to wage for double overtime&nbsp;<br>worked.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1034px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft616"><i>min_paid_break</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1034px;left:315px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">int</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1034px;left:477px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft611">Minimum time to start paid break</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:261px;left:97px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft617"><b>GET&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:261px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft618"><i><b>/api/v3.5/export/{customerid}/{locationid}?data_type=config&amp;sub_data_type=payroll_profil</b></i><b>e</b></p>
</div>

<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft630">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft630">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:591px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft630">Working with the Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;63</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:153px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft631">2.4.3&nbsp;&nbsp;Employee Labor Data</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:186px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft632">Employee Labor data provides the output of work tracked across the time period specified.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:280px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft633">Relevant parameters</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:320px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft634"><b>Parameter</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:320px;left:484px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft634"><b>Description</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:366px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft635"><i><b>start_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:393px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft632">(Basic)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:366px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft6310">Specifies the starting point for the export. This will include all employee and labor data&nbsp;<br>for this date and onward until&nbsp;<b>end_date</b>&nbsp;(if applicable).</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:411px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft636"><i>This is mandatory if not using the&nbsp;<b>delta</b>&nbsp;parameters.</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:438px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft634"><b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:484px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft635"><i><b>end_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:511px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft632">(Basic)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:484px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft6310">Specifies the end date for the export. If applied this will be the end of the date range and&nbsp;<br>include all employee and labor data up to and including this date.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:529px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft6310">If&nbsp;<b>end_date</b>&nbsp;is not specified then the export will return all indexed employee and labor&nbsp;<br>data up until the moment that the request to the API was made.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:574px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft634"><b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:620px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft635"><i><b>delta_from_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:647px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft632">(Advanced)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:620px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft6310">These parameters should only be used when doing incremental export updates&nbsp;<br>throughout the day such as for integrators updating data live. If using delta parameters,&nbsp;<br>do not use the startDate and endDate parameters.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:693px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft635"><i><b>delta_from_time</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:720px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft632">(Advanced)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:803px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft637"><i>Labor&nbsp;</i>object</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:844px;left:145px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft634"><b>Attribute&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:844px;left:332px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft634"><b>Type&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:844px;left:542px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft634"><b>Additional information&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:890px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft636"><i>labor_id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:890px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft632">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:890px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft6310">Id built with these two params: [Clock In Object ID]_[Job&nbsp;<br>Title ID]</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:954px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft636"><i>employee_id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:954px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft632">int</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:954px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft632">Employee Qu ID</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1000px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft636"><i>job_id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1000px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft632">int</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1000px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft632">Job Title ID</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1046px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft636"><i>payroll_profile_id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1046px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft632">int</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1046px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft632">Payroll Profile ID</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:225px;left:97px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft638"><b>GET&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:225px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft635"><i><b>/api/v3.5/export/{customerid}/{locationid}?data_type=labor</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:697px;left:290px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft6310">Using the&nbsp;<b>delta</b>&nbsp;fields will return data that can be “volatile” in that the data&nbsp;<br>could be altered after the initial polling and should always be reconciled with a&nbsp;<br>standard lookback request to ensure the information is complete.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:694px;left:260px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft639"></p>
</div>

<p style="position:absolute;top:955px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft667">2.5&nbsp;&nbsp;Accounting Data</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:991px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft6611">Integrators use the Data API for accounting functions can access data related to cash tills, over/under and paid in/<br>out data that is essential to balancing the books at the end of the day and pay period.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1053px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft669">2.5.1&nbsp;&nbsp;Closed and Reconciled Tills</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1086px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft668">This request provides all closed and reconciled cash tills for the selected location and date range.</p>
