<div id="page67-div" style="position:relative;width:892px;height:1262px;">
<img width="892" height="1262" src="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/target067.png" alt="background image">
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft670">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft670">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:591px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft670">Working with the Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;67</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:219px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft671">Relevant parameters</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:259px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft672"><b>Parameter</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:259px;left:484px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft672"><b>Description</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:305px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft673"><i><b>start_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:332px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">(Basic)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:305px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft678">Specifies the starting point for the export. This will include all till data for this date and&nbsp;<br>onward until&nbsp;<b>end_date</b>&nbsp;(if applicable).</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:350px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft675"><i>This is mandatory if not using the&nbsp;<b>delta</b>&nbsp;parameters.</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:377px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft672"><b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:423px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft673"><i><b>end_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:450px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">(Basic)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:423px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft678">Specifies the end date for the export. If applied this will be the end of the date range and&nbsp;<br>include all till data up to and including this date.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:468px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft678">If&nbsp;<b>end_date</b>&nbsp;is not specified then the export will return all indexed employee and labor&nbsp;<br>data up until the moment that the request to the API was made.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:513px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft672"><b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:559px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft673"><i><b>delta_from_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:586px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">(Advanced)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:559px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft678">These parameters should only be used when doing incremental export updates&nbsp;<br>throughout the day such as for integrators updating data live. If using delta parameters,&nbsp;<br>do not use the startDate and endDate parameters.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:632px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft673"><i><b>delta_from_time</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:659px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">(Advanced)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:742px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft671">Tills object</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:782px;left:145px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft672"><b>Attribute&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:782px;left:332px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft672"><b>Type&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:782px;left:581px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft672"><b>Description</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:828px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft675"><i>till_id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:828px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:828px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:875px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft675"><i>till_name</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:875px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:875px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:921px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft675"><i>cash_drawer_id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:921px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">int</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:921px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:967px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft675"><i>terminal_id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:967px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">int</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:967px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1013px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft675"><i>till_claim_date_time</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1013px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1013px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">Format: yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss (Store local time)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1059px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft675"><i>till_close_date_time</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1059px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1059px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft674">Format: yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss (Store local time)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:164px;left:97px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft676"><b>GET&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:164px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft673"><i><b>/api/v3.5/export/{customerid}/{locationid}?data_type=tills</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:636px;left:290px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft678">Using the&nbsp;<b>delta</b>&nbsp;fields will return data that can be “volatile” in that the data&nbsp;<br>could be altered after the initial polling and should always be reconciled with a&nbsp;<br>standard lookback request to ensure the information is complete.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:632px;left:260px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft677"></p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:347px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft681"><i>skims</i></p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:347px;left:360px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft683"><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html">Skim</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:347px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft686">Skims are performed to temporarily reduce the amount&nbsp;<br>of cash on a till. The main difference&nbsp;<br>between Skims and Paid outs is that Skims do not affect&nbsp;<br>the till’s expected cash.</p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:464px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft724">2.5.2&nbsp;&nbsp;Deposits</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:497px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft7212">Store managers create deposits to declare cash that was extracted from the store and deposited in the bank. Each&nbsp;<br>cash deposit is linked to a list of reconciled tills. Deposits can be edited and deleted in EI.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:608px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft726">Relevant parameters</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:648px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft727"><b>Parameter</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:648px;left:484px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft727"><b>Description</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:694px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft728"><i><b>start_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:721px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft725">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:694px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft7212">Specifies the starting point for the export. This will include all deposit data created on&nbsp;<br>this date and onward until&nbsp;<b>end_date</b>&nbsp;(if applicable).</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:739px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft727"><b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:786px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft728"><i><b>end_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:813px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft725">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:786px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft7212">Specifies the end date for the export. If applied this will be the end of the date range and&nbsp;<br>include all deposit data created up to and including this date.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:831px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft7212">If&nbsp;<b>end_date</b>&nbsp;is not specified then the export will return all indexed deposit data up until&nbsp;<br>the moment that the request to the API was made.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:876px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft727"><b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:937px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft726">Deposit object</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:977px;left:160px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft727"><b>Attribute&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:977px;left:348px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft727"><b>Type&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:977px;left:543px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft727"><b>Additional Information&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1024px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft729"><i>id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1024px;left:307px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft725">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1024px;left:444px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft725">The cash deposit id</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:554px;left:97px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft7210"><b>GET</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:554px;left:123px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft727"><b>&nbsp;<i>/api/v3.5/export/{customerid}/{locationid}?data_type=deposits</i></b></p>
</div>

<div id="page73-div" style="position:relative;width:892px;height:1262px;">
<img width="892" height="1262" src="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/target073.png" alt="background image">
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft730">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft730">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:591px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft730">Working with the Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;73</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft731"><i>date_time_deposit</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:307px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft732">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:162px;left:444px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft736">The date and time when the deposit was made at the&nbsp;<br>bank, according to the employee adding the deposit&nbsp;<br>entry.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:225px;left:444px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft732">Format: yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss (Store Local Time)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:271px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft731"><i>date_time_created</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:271px;left:307px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft732">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:271px;left:444px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft736">The date and time when the deposit was created in Qu.&nbsp;<br>This is the date used by the request start and end date&nbsp;<br>filters.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:334px;left:444px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft732">Format: yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss (Store Local Time)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:380px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft731"><i>deposit_number</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:380px;left:307px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft732">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:380px;left:444px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft732">Reference number provided by the user</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:426px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft731"><i>expected_deposit</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:426px;left:307px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft732">decimal</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:426px;left:444px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft736">Total sum of all linked Till’s Actual Cash, minus the tills&nbsp;<br>starting cash (tills.reconciliation.actual_cash -&nbsp;<br>tills.<i>starting_cash</i>)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:509px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft731"><i>deposited_cash</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:509px;left:307px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft732">decimal</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:509px;left:444px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft732">The actual cash amount that was deposited</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:555px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft731"><i>comments</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:555px;left:307px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft732">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:555px;left:444px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft736">Additional comments provided by the user in regards to&nbsp;<br>the deposit</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:619px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft731"><i>tills</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:619px;left:307px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft732">Collection of&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:637px;left:307px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft733"><a href="file:///C:/Users/Evan%20McFadden/Downloads/index.html">till_id</a></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:637px;left:343px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft732">&nbsp;(string)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:619px;left:444px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft732">List of reconciled tills that were linked to this deposit</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:692px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft734">Created Date vs. Deposit Date</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:719px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft737">The Qu system lists deposits based on the date of creation in the system, not the date of the actual deposit to the&nbsp;<br>bank. This is because deposits may be made to the bank in non-consecutive days and requires user entry to&nbsp;<br>confirm. For example, some businesses may add the deposits the next day everyday except Sunday, and some may&nbsp;<br>log them right before the end of a pay period.&nbsp;<b>This is important to note as the parameters for start and end date&nbsp;<br>will return the deposits created in the time period, not necessarily the deposits made in that time period.</b></p>
</div>

<p style="position:absolute;top:985px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft745">2.5.3&nbsp;&nbsp;Over/Under Data</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1018px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft7410">Over/Under data provides the difference in expected cash till and payments vs. the actual recorded over a period of&nbsp;<br>time.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1075px;left:97px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft747"><b>GET&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1075px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft748"><i><b>/api/v3.5/export/{customerid}/{locationid}?data_type=over_under</b></i></p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft750">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft750">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:591px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft750">Working with the Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;75</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:153px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft751">Relevant parameters</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:193px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft752"><b>Parameter</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:193px;left:484px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft752"><b>Description</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:239px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft753"><i><b>start_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:266px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft754">(Basic)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:239px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft7511">Specifies the starting point for the export. This will include all employee and labor data&nbsp;<br>for this date and onward until&nbsp;<b>end_date</b>&nbsp;(if applicable).</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:284px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft755"><i>This is mandatory if not using the&nbsp;<b>delta</b>&nbsp;parameters.</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:311px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft752"><b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:357px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft753"><i><b>end_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:384px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft754">(Basic)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:357px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft7511">Specifies the end date for the export. If applied this will be the end of the date range and&nbsp;<br>include all employee and labor data up to and including this date.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:402px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft7511">If&nbsp;<b>end_date</b>&nbsp;is not specified then the export will return all indexed employee and labor&nbsp;<br>data up until the moment that the request to the API was made.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:447px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft752"><b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:509px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft751">Over/Under object</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:549px;left:154px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft752"><b>Attribute&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:549px;left:529px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft752"><b>Type&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:595px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft755"><i>over_under</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:595px;left:295px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft754">decimal</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:657px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft751">Example over/under response</p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:908px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft758">0.01</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:926px;left:102px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft7512">&nbsp; }<br>}</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1003px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft759">2.5.4&nbsp;&nbsp;Paid In/Out Data</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1036px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft754">Paid In/Out provides a log of pay ins and pay outs across a given time period.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1075px;left:97px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft7510"><b>GET&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1075px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft753"><i><b>/api/v3.5/export/{customerid}/{locationid}?data_type=paid_inout</b></i></p>

<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:393px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft760">Qu Data Export API</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:70px;left:739px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft760">Integrations</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:1171px;left:591px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft760">Working with the Data Export API&nbsp; –&nbsp;&nbsp;76</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:152px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft767">In addition to the listing of all objects, the response data includes a running total amount of both pay ins and pay&nbsp;<br>outs separately.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:213px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft762">Relevant parameters</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:253px;left:126px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft763"><b>Parameter</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:253px;left:484px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft763"><b>Description</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:299px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft764"><i><b>start_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:299px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft767">Specifies the starting point for the export. This will include all pay ins and outs for this&nbsp;<br>date and onward until&nbsp;<b>end_date</b>&nbsp;(if applicable).</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:344px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft765"><i>This is mandatory if not using the&nbsp;<b>delta</b>&nbsp;parameters.</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:371px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft763"><b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:417px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft764"><i><b>end_date</b></i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:417px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft767">Specifies the end date for the export. If applied this will be the end of the date range and&nbsp;<br>include all pay ins and outs up to and including this date.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:462px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft767">If&nbsp;<b>end_date</b>&nbsp;is not specified then the export will return all indexed employee and labor&nbsp;<br>data up until the moment that the request to the API was made.</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:507px;left:247px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft763"><b>Format</b>: MMDDYYYY</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:569px;left:85px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft766"><b>Paid In/Out object</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:609px;left:145px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft763"><b>Attribute&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:609px;left:332px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft763"><b>Type&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:609px;left:542px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft763"><b>Additional Information&nbsp;</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:655px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft765"><i>applied_at</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:655px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft761">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:655px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft761">Format: yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss (Store Local Time)</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:701px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft765"><i>employee_id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:701px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft761">int</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:701px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft761">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:747px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft765"><i>amount</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:747px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft761">decimal</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:747px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft763"><b>This can be a negative value.</b></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:793px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft765"><i>paid_inout_id</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:793px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft761">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:793px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft761">Paid In/Out Reason ID – Changed from int to string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:839px;left:95px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft765"><i>reason_text</i></p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:839px;left:277px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft761">string</p>
<p style="position:absolute;top:839px;left:441px;white-space:nowrap" class="ft761">Paid In/Out note</p>
</div>
